SELECT ?date ?time ?coordinates ?species ?stranded ?sampleSize
    WHERE {
        ?obs a sosa:Observation ;
             dct:date "10/07/2011" ;
             dct:time "09:00" ;
             geojson:geometry [ geojson:coordinates Unknown ] ;
             ns1:strandedJellyfish 1 ;
             iliad:sampleSizeValue "    iliad:sampleSizeValue "30-60" .
        BIND("60Rhopilema_nomadica" AS ?species)
    }

        ?obs a sosa:Observation ;
             dct:date "11/07/2012" ;
             dct:time "16:00" ;
             geojson:geometry [ geojson:coordinates Unknown ] ;
             ns1:strandedJellyfish 1 ;
             iliad:sampleSizeValue "    iliad:sampleSizeValue "Oct-30" .
        BIND("666666666711232Phyllorhiza_punctata" AS ?species)
    }

        ?obs a sosa:Observation ;
             dct:date "Unknown" ;
             dct:time "Unknown" ;
             geojson:geometry [ geojson:coordinates Unknown ] ;
             ns1:strandedJellyfish Unknown ;
             iliad:sampleSizeValue "Unknown" .
        BIND("2511232Pelagia_noctiluca" AS ?species)
    }
